# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="8d3d6-102">Membri obsoleti in .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3d6-102">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8d3d6-103">In questo articolo sono elencati i membri di tipo che sono obsoleti in.NET Framework 4.5 e versioni successive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3d6-103">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8d3d6-104">I membri di tipo sono raggruppati in base all'assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3d6-104">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8d3d6-105">In questo articolo non sono elencati i membri dei tipi obsoleti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3d6-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8d3d6-106">Per un elenco dei tipi obsoleti, vedere [Tipi obsoleti](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3d6-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>
